AI Conversations is Giving Website Search a Higher IQ ","intro":"The website search and content discovery company’s newest feature helps modernize website experiences, enabling visitors to interact conversationally and receive clear, trustworthy answers powered exclusively by your website content. Interview with CEO Helena Rebane.","content":"\u003chr /\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eWebsite search has come a long way, baby. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eYup. We all remember those dreaded days of \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://medium.com/next-century-user-experience/the-dreaded-boolean-search-413fa757a81c\"\u003eBoolean mechanics\u003c/a\u003e. Back when we fished with keywords, and the use of an \u003ci\u003e“and,”\u003c/i\u003e \u003ci\u003e“or\u003c/i\u003e,” or \u003ci\u003e“not”\u003c/i\u003e could doom you to a barrage of irrelevant results.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eSearch design improved, thankfully. And so did user behavior. But the traditional model continued to suffer from its litany of links, forcing website visitors to comb through results to find what they were after. Not fun.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eGen AI has changed all of that, specifically with the advent of \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://aws.amazon.com/what-is/retrieval-augmented-generation/\"\u003eRAG – Retrieval Augmented Generation\u003c/a\u003e. Unlike ChatGPT and other AI engines, RAG principles enable a search service to index and vectorize the content that’s just on your website. When a query is made, the system only searches the data on your website and uses an LLM to generate a natural response.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAnd \u003ci\u003epresto\u003c/i\u003e. More accurate answers because it’s limited to your cache of content. Fewer hallucinations because it’s not trained on misinformation or bad patterns.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eThis is where \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.addsearch.com/\"\u003eAddSearch\u003c/a\u003e, a Finland-based SaaS company that focuses exclusively on website search and content discovery, is evolving the experience. The company has over 1,800 customers (including thyssenkrupp, Lysol, and Bitnami) that utilize its \u003ca href=\"AI%20Search\"\u003eAI Search\u003c/a\u003e to personalize search experiences and optimize performance via analytics. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eNow, AddSearch’s newest feature, \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.addsearch.com/ai-conversations/\"\u003eAI Conversations,\u003c/a\u003e is taking things to the next level. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eUnlike other market solutions, including AddSearch’s popular \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.addsearch.com/ai-answers/\"\u003eAI Answers\u003c/a\u003e service (which delivers single, direct responses to individual questions), AI Conversations provides coherent answers by continually reading your company’s library of web content in real-time. This gives visitors a more intuitive content discovery experience where they can interact conversationally and receive clear, trustworthy, non-hallucinatory answers.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAI Conversations also provides a critical layer of conversational context. This is a big advantage, as it enables website visitors to ask follow-up questions, seek clarification, and explore topics naturally without starting over. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cfigure class=\"image image_resized\" style=\"width:85.41%\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/02/image-1772149994944.png\" alt=\"A screenshot of a computer\n\nAI-generated content may be incorrect.\" /\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"text-small\" style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003eSource: AddSearch website\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAI Conversations is ideal for content-heavy websites, surfacing a clean UI for natural, conversational interaction. You can also toggle seamlessly between conversational and traditional search interfaces. It doesn’t require a site rebuild or fancy refactor, and you can be live in days with technical support and fast setup for any CMS via AddSearch’s Crawler or API. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eFor marketers, site search continues to be a vital part of a well-balanced digital strategy. \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://segmentify.com/blog/on-site-search-discovery-statistics/\"\u003eAccording to Segmentify,\u003c/a\u003e roughly 43% of all retail customers hit the search bar first when they arrive on a site. But as one study suggested, \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://segmentify.com/blog/on-site-search-discovery-statistics/\"\u003e39% of websites fail\u003c/a\u003e to properly support non-product searches. This is where AI can bridge the gap for legacy search experiences.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eEven as website visitors shift from keyword searches to asking full questions with AI-powered answers, many websites are struggling to keep up. This is where AddSearch’s AI Conversations is helping brands and organizations accelerate the modernization of their website search and content discovery. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cfigure class=\"image image_resized\" style=\"width:32.81%\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/02/image-1772149994818.png\" alt=\"A person with dark hair and a purple background\n\nAI-generated content may be incorrect.\" /\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"text-small\" style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003eAddSearch CEO Helena Rebane. Source: LinkedIn\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eI recently caught up with AddSearch’s CEO, \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/helenarebane/\"\u003eHelena Rebane.\u003c/a\u003e She's been in the pilot's chair for over five years, navigating the company through the bright horizons and stormy skies of generative AI. She explained why this next chapter with AI Conversations is a game-changer – not just for the market, but for her company's trajectory.\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"why-traditional-search-feels-‘broken’\"\u003eWhy traditional search feels ‘broken’\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003eSince 2013, AddSearch has worked at the edge of the search field, studying how user behavior influences expectations. The rise of conversational AI is now repositioning the baseline.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“We’ve always seen that whatever search behavior is happening with Google or different search platforms, it influences what people expect to happen on websites,” she said. “This is what is happening with AI as well. And such behaviors are changing with conversational AI, and this is now what users are increasingly expecting on websites.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eArguably, websites have evolved. But what’s really changing is the consumer’s search behavior. Thanks to ChatGPT and Gemini, relying on keywords has become passé, and more users have become accustomed to dumping detailed questions into chatbot fields and expecting context-aware answers. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eNow they expect it from search, and when it’s not there, it could be a signal that a site isn’t as modern as its competitors. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“The traffic that we get on websites is increasingly coming from ChatGPT and similar platforms,” Helena said. “We assume that when they are using these kinds of tools, and they come on a website, they want to continue to have the same kind of experience. If you have a very outdated keyword search on your website, then the whole website experience suddenly feels very outdated.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003chr /\u003e\u003ch4 style=\"text-align:center\" id=\"-\"\u003e \u003c/h4\u003e\u003ch4 style=\"text-align:center\" id=\"“we’ve-always-seen-that-whatever-search-behavior-is-happening-with-google-or-different-search-platforms,-it-influences-what-people-expect-to-happen-on-websites.-this-is-what-is-happening-with-ai-as-well.”\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:rgb(48,49,61)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003e\u003cmark class=\"marker-yellow\"\u003e“We’ve always seen that whatever search behavior is happening with Google or different search platforms, it influences what people expect to happen on websites. This is what is happening with AI as well.”\u003c/mark\u003e\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h4\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003chr /\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eThis is why the search experience feels broken – creating friction, slower discovery, and missed opportunities to engage visitors. At the same time, Helena pointed out the compounding effects of \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://neilpatel.com/blog/zero-click-searches/\"\u003ezero‑click searches \u003c/a\u003eand AI answer engines, which are changing the value perception of site search.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“There’s a big change happening for websites, because in addition to what they see with their site search behavior, they also see this massive decrease in traffic to websites overall,” she explained. “I think this is a big signal, and website owners are saying, ‘Hey, there’s a lot of change happening, and we need to do something. What are the options?'\"\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAs Helena told me, evolving site search could be a salve for battling engagement erosion, and it provides some connective tissue to the broader AI motion. She still thinks we’re in an early adoption phase – and that many companies might miss the boat and struggle to catch up. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eThis is where AddSearch’s AI Conversations can close the gap, bringing conversational content discovery directly into an organization’s website. It also addresses the long-standing challenge of fragmented web content by consolidating information from multiple pages and sections into actionable responses.\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"turning-questions-into-clear-answers-and-insights\"\u003eTurning questions into clear answers and insights\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003eAs mentioned, the central benefit of focusing AI Conversations on a company’s sovereign website content is trust. Visitors get consistent, on-brand answers instead of weirdly hallucinated replies or grossly inaccurate third-party information. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eBut Helena noted how this technology is also providing greater visibility into content gaps and quality issues – and that knowledge is invaluable when it comes to understanding customer behavior and optimizing performance.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“Even if you’re not interested in improving your own site search experience, then one of the ways you can use these kinds of tools on your website is to see what people are asking about your products,” she said. “You can review every question people have asked in a search session, and you can see every answer AI provided.” \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eBingo. With a RAG approach like this, you know exactly what the source is. That means if you have wrong or outdated content, then your AI answers will be based on that. Not only does this allow you to improve your site search results, but the insight extends into the realm of the answer engines – which are indexing your site content to arm their results.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“You can assume that if your site search gives you the wrong answer based on your website content, then it’s likely that ChatGPT will do the same,” Helena reinforced. “So it could harm your business beyond just your website. So using these tools is a great opportunity to become aware of these problems and fix them.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eIn other words, AI Conversations doesn’t just modernize search – it becomes a feedback loop for optimizing your content strategy and brand accuracy.\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"‘landing-and-expanding’-with-cmss-and-agencies\"\u003e‘Landing and expanding’ with CMSs and agencies\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003eRather than tying conversational search to a single platform, AddSearch built AI Conversations to sit cleanly on top of existing digital experience stacks. This includes the all-important content authority of a CMS as a foundational layer. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“We work with any CMS as an agnostic solution,” Helena said, “and we have integrations to \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://cmscritic.com/products/wordpress\"\u003eWordPress\u003c/a\u003e and \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://cmscritic.com/products/shopify\"\u003eShopify\u003c/a\u003e as well.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAs a channel conduit, agencies have also been part of AddSearch’s delivery. As enterprises increasingly rely on their agency partners to translate the value and select the best technologies to enhance their websites, AddSearch is emerging as a scalable, performant, and reliable solution. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“We work very closely with digital and marketing agencies all over the world, and there’s been a lot of interest from them,” Helena explained. “Many organizations know that they need to do something, but they don’t know what. And usually that’s when you turn to consultants, right? We also work with agencies that are doing background research to find the best solutions for the customers they represent. The response we hear is that there’s a lot of eagerness to find solutions that will improve the website experience.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAddSearch also offers an \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.addsearch.com/partners/\"\u003eagency partner program\u003c/a\u003e, which focuses on supporting the entire lifecycle from sales to implementation to optimization.\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"from-answers-to-actions:-roi,-agents,-and-security\"\u003eFrom answers to actions: ROI, agents, and security\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003eHelena was clear that the next evolutionary step for AI and websites will be measured not just in user satisfaction, but in delivering tangible business outcomes.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“We see several things happening, but the first thing is that organizations are looking for ROI,” she said. “This is something that we’re also focusing on by helping our customers win business with our solutions. It’s about monetization of the conversational tools. So being able to drive business and track ROI is definitely a big deal on all sides.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eI asked Helena how the emergence of AI agents is potentially shifting the trajectory. As she said, AddSearch’s focus is leading naturally into more agentic experiences, where their AI experiences don’t just answer questions, but they help visitors accomplish tasks.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“We’re focused on agentic behavior that’s not just giving you answers, but actually doing things for you,” she responded. “Maybe you want to get something done when you visit a website, or as a website owner, you want to automate tasks that assist your visitors. That’s something that’s going to grow a lot, and we’re going to focus on that as well.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eUnderpinning all of this is a strong emphasis on trust and transparency, specifically as it relates to the all-important questions of security and data privacy. AddSearch already meets \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.addsearch.com/blog/soc-2-trust-in-the-digital-realm/\"\u003eSOC 2 certification\u003c/a\u003e, emphasizing its dedication to maintaining fierce data protection standards. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eHelena doesn’t want security to be a black box. To that end, she advocates for greater transparency – particularly as AI transforms application architectures and the underlying infrastructure.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“We’re putting further emphasis on security and showing the customer the security part a little more, because we see that this is a huge concern,” Helena said. “How is my data being used? How is AI still providing the right answers? We want to provide as much transparency about this and give customers confidence that their information is being used properly – and that AI can be relied on with their website.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"pricing\"\u003ePricing\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003eAddSearch is solid SaaS, and as I said, relatively easy to add to any site or CMS. I won’t say it’s the \u003ci\u003eeasiest\u003c/i\u003e (vis-à-vis “one-line” JavaScript solutions), so you’ll need to engage with their technical team on the details. But they stand by having you up and running quickly – within 1-2 weeks, or in many cases, just a couple of days.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eI like the \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.addsearch.com/pricing/\"\u003eclear pricing\u003c/a\u003e that AddSearch provides for its search product, which effectively scales based on features. It starts with \u003cstrong\u003eCore\u003c/strong\u003e at $119/month and elevates to \u003cstrong\u003eGrowth\u003c/strong\u003e at $299/month. There’s also an \u003cstrong\u003eAdvanced\u003c/strong\u003e plan for more robust sites, which includes a custom search UI, SLA, and content and product recommendations. That runs for $599/month. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAI Answers\u003c/strong\u003e has a starting price of $8,400/year, and \u003cstrong\u003eAI Conversations\u003c/strong\u003e currently has no price guidance. You’ll need to connect with their sales team for a demo to inquire about custom pricing, but the AI Answer baseline should give you an idea of what to expect. \u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"the-verdict\"\u003eThe verdict\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003eAI-powered website search and discovery is a no-brainer – and an easy win to enhance any website. As consumers drift toward AI answer engines like ChatGPT and Perplexity, having a congruous experience on your own site will help meet modern expectations, reduce friction, and ultimately drive more conversions. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAddSearch’s AI Conversations provides dynamite value with its conversational context. This is a big advantage, as it enables website visitors to ask follow-up questions, seek clarification, and explore topics naturally without starting over. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eThe players in the site search category are expanding, and I’ve been tracking several vendors with solid solutions. Some of the core features are becoming more commoditized, and all offer analytics and other goodies to sweeten the search experience. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAI is clearly the game-changer, so tune into how it's being harnessed, where your data lives, and the level of visibility and observability a platform provides. You'll also want to inquire about the agentic roadmap and what kind of automation is available and forthcoming. For example, executing adjustments based on specific analytics results or optimizing an aspect of search criteria via an agent workflow could be great use cases.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eThere are standout reasons to select specific vendors – particularly around considerations like scalability, compliance, and off-the-shelf CMS or DXP integrations that are sometimes available as a co-sell. These are factors to pay attention to when evaluating options.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan class=\"text-big\"\u003e\u003cmark class=\"marker-yellow\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMy recommendation:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/mark\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAddSearch has been around the block, giving them more market insight around search experience. They have a proven track record and solid market footprint – and happy customers based on their G2 Reviews. I tend to highlight the “Best Support” and “Best ROI” as true examples of how a product earns its keep.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eIf you’re considering an upgrade to your website search (which, if you haven’t, you should), this is a great product that’s competitively priced. Choice: New Survey from MemberWise Puts Umbraco CMS on Top for Membership Organizations","intro":"The 2026 Digital Excellence Report reveals that the open source CMS is the primary content management system used to create digital experiences for membership organizations focused on retention and growth.","content":"\u003chr /\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eIf you don’t have a membership card in your wallet or purse, you probably have a letter in your mailbox from an organization or association you belong to.  \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eExample: I've supported the \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.sierraclub.org/\"\u003eSierra Club\u003c/a\u003e for years. I'm still fighting off the \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.aarp.org/\"\u003eAARP\u003c/a\u003e, but I sense it coming. I’ve heard they offer some pretty great discounts.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eThere are thousands of these bodies across the globe, composed of millions of people from all walks of life. This includes trade and professional associations, labor organizations, social enterprises – the list goes on.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAs such, these communities of interest are big. So big, in fact, that there’s an organization dedicated to supporting, connecting, and providing the category “glue” for membership-based entities. It’s called \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://memberwise.org.uk/\"\u003eMemberWise\u003c/a\u003e, an independent network for international membership and association professionals. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eIt’s free to become a member of MemberWise (making the whole thing a little meta), and it currently represents over 8,000 individuals working from more than 2,500 UK membership organizations and associations. This includes the British Medical Association, the Royal College of Nursing, and the IET. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eFrom a mission perspective, MemberWise enriches its community with access to best-practice guidance, expert knowledge, resources (like webinars), and networking events designed to help professionals improve member engagement, retention, and growth. It also features a \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://memberwise.org.uk/how-to-become-a-memberwise-recognised-supplier/\"\u003eRecognized Supplier Directory\u003c/a\u003e with over 170 technology and service providers.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eEvery few years, the MemberWise Network conducts its \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://memberwise.org.uk/dx/\"\u003eDigital Excellence Research Project,\u003c/a\u003e a survey-based initiative that offers relevant perspectives on the digital tools, activities, and strategies being employed within the membership and association sector. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eThe research, which is independently written by the network and contains statistically significant findings, is published in its \u003cstrong\u003eDigital Excellence Report\u003c/strong\u003e – delivering a clear view of new and emerging trends that can help drive organizational goals. The facts and figures are often used to bolster business cases and increase internal support when facilitating operational or strategic changes.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cimg style=\"width:70.51%\" src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/02/image-1772055247658.jpeg\" alt=\"A close-up of a logo\n\nAI-generated content may be incorrect.\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"text-small\" style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003eSource: MemberWise website\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://memberwise.org.uk/dx/\"\u003eThe 2026 edition was just released\u003c/a\u003e, and it reveals some interesting data points about content management systems for membership bodies and associations. For robust entities, having a secure, scalable, and reliable CMS is vital to powering communication and engagement through various channels – specifically an association’s website.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eFor the fifth consecutive year, \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"http://www.umbraco.com/\"\u003eUmbraco\u003c/a\u003e was cited as the number one web content management system platform cited by medium and large membership organizations for developing websites and digital experiences, specifically to support their efforts in retaining and attracting new members and growing revenue.\u003cspan style=\"color:#212121\"\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eThat last piece is critical, and the 2026 report doubles down on the compelling need for the sector to engage, retain, and grow memberships. It also highlights the challenge of rising costs and the mandate to counter it, so membership bodies can continue delivering services both online and offline.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cfigure class=\"image image_resized\" style=\"width:43.7%\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/02/image-1772055247861.png\" alt=\"A person with short hair wearing a blue shirt\n\nAI-generated content may be incorrect.\" /\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"text-small\" style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003eJacob Howell. Source: LinkedIn\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“We’re delighted to see that the majority of medium and large membership organizations continue to choose the Umbraco CMS platform to support their member acquisition, engagement, and revenue growth,” said \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/howelljacob/\"\u003eJacob Howell,\u003c/a\u003e Umbraco’s UK Partner Manager.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAccording to the report’s author and MemberWise Network Founder and Chair \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/memberwise/\"\u003eRichard Gott,\u003c/a\u003e growth is now a requirement for all membership bodies – and it’s increasingly dependent on delivering engaging and value-driven digital journeys and experiences.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cimg style=\"width:43.21%\" src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/02/image-1772055247878.png\" alt=\"A close-up of a person smiling\n\nAI-generated content may be incorrect.\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"text-small\" style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003eRichard Gott. Source: LinkedIn\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“This is why the report focuses on the performance of websites, digital publications, apps, and the technologies that membership organizations and their digital agencies are selecting to create those experiences,” he said. “Over the past five years, we have observed membership organizations and associations adopting more sophisticated content management systems to optimize – and increasingly personalize – online member journeys, engagement, experiences, and purchases.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"key-findings\"\u003eKey findings\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003eThe 2026 MemberWise Digital Excellence Report was based on survey responses from 480 individuals across the UK membership and association sector. Segments were defined around subscription revenue, from small to medium to large. The figures are available in the report.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eThere were some notable findings in this year’s research. For example, new member acquisition, engagement, and growth continue to be key priorities for membership organizations, along with increasing revenue from non-subscription activities such as conferences and continuous professional development.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAdditionally, the \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://memberwise.org.uk/influence100/\"\u003elargest 100 membership bodies in the UK\u003c/a\u003e are now spending almost $340 million (£250 million) per year on digital technologies and web-based solutions – a massive investment that gives this market vertical real buying power. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAs stated, Umbraco is the CMS most commonly used by medium and large membership bodies. But here’s the kicker: more organizations than ever stated that they are satisfied with their CMS (+18%) and are now spending between 2% and 5% of total annual budgets on related technologies.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eOther layers of the stack are feeling the lift. For example, association management systems and focused industry CRMs are continuing to see increased website integration (+5%), and the path to integration is accelerating. Additionally, a greater number of membership bodies are measuring engagement via website and member portal activity, suggesting that analytics and insights are becoming a central imperative.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e59% of respondents also said that they’re using their CMS to personalize digital experiences for online members. In tandem, more organizations are personalizing content based on qualifying data such as areas of interest or geographic location. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eFinally, AI is becoming a more visible mandate. According to the research, adoption of AI-powered website functionality has increased by 21% over the past two years, suggesting that more associations are trusting AI in their digital workflows and operations – and that trend is likely to grow.\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"umbraco’s-agency-partners-activate-growth-and-success\"\u003eUmbraco’s agency partners activate growth and success\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003eOne of the key pillars of Umbraco’s success is its hard-earned, highly-engaged community of more than 250,000 developers and users – buoyed by its well-established global partner network of digital agencies. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eThese diverse shops offer both vertical and horizontal specializations, and several have implemented solutions for membership organizations and associations. According to Jacob Howell, Umbraco’s performance in the 2026 Digital Excellence Report is a testament to the company’s digital agency partners, including \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.cantarus.com/\"\u003eCantarus\u003c/a\u003e, \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.wearewattle.com/clients/clients/\"\u003eWattle\u003c/a\u003e, \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.teambluelight.com/case-studies/?page=1\"\u003eBluelight\u003c/a\u003e, and \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.msqdx.co.uk/en/about\"\u003eMSQ DX\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAs he said, these teams have turned ambitious digital strategies into exceptional digital experiences, powered by Umbraco. “We’re proud to provide them with an open-source platform that gives them flexibility to integrate additional technologies, whenever required, while offering an intuitive interface for content editors at membership organizations.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cfigure class=\"image image_resized\" style=\"width:83.5%\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/02/screenshot-2026-02-25-at-4.png\" /\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"text-small\" style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003eSource: Cantarus website's membership section\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eCantarus, Umbraco’s first transatlantic Platinum partner, has been an official part of the MemberWise Network for over a decade. The agency often shares thought leadership, success stories, and best practices for building websites and digital solutions that help organizations to engage and retain members. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eBoasting more than seventy membership organizations as clients, Cantarus is considered a market leader in the sector, having built websites and digital experiences for The Royal College of Physicians, British Computer Society, and The Law Society of England and Wales.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“We’ve been heavily invested in the membership sector for over a decade, and it’s now our most important individual sector,” said Cantarus CEO \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/leeadams/\"\u003eLee Adams.\u003c/a\u003e “When you’re responsible for the performance, stability, and security of a membership organization’s site, it’s important to have full confidence in the technologies selected to build it.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cfigure class=\"image image_resized\" style=\"width:42.83%\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/02/image-1772055247926.png\" alt=\"A person in a suit\n\nAI-generated content may be incorrect.\" /\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"text-small\" style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003eLee Adams. Source: LinkedIn\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAdams went on to explain how Umbraco allows digital agencies like Cantarus to build websites and digital experiences that are tailored to the immediate requirements of membership organizations – with the flexibility and scalability to extend the platform as they grow. In essence, it’s future-proofing for a shifting landscape.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“Because Umbraco is a powerful open source platform, we can tap into that creative ecosystem to offer clients a lower-cost implementation with no risk of vendor lock-in,” he continued, “and without limiting their technology options as members’ digital preferences evolve.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eComplementing the report is MemberWise’s signature event, the \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/showcase/digitalexcellence2026/posts/?feedView=all\"\u003e2026 Digital Excellence Conference \u0026amp; Exhibition\u003c/a\u003e, which exclusively focuses on the membership and association sector.\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"why-it-matters\"\u003eWhy it matters\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003eAs “The Friendly CMS,” it’s no surprise that Umbraco is a go-to CMS for organizations that focus on building and engaging with vibrant communities. At a granular level, this is a testament to Umbraco’s flexibility, reliability, and ease of use – as well as its end-to-end features for enabling rich functionality across modern digital experiences. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eMemberships and associations might seem like a niche market, but it’s a much larger segment than you might have realized. Clearly, Umbraco has endeavored to unpack the member journey and elevate the experience in a way that’s endearing to both its partner agencies and end customers – allowing them to build greater retention and loyalty while powering marketing strategies to attract new members.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cmark class=\"marker-yellow\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMy recommendation:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/mark\u003e If you’re a membership or association, take a look at this MemberWise research and use it as a point of validation. While this is a regionally specific study, the data regarding content management and digital experiences is extensible. There are many CMSes that could potentially meet diverse requirements, but Umbraco and its partners have invested deeply in the goals and outcomes for this segment, and continue to push forward in areas like AI and personalization. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAs an open source platform, Umbraco also brings its own community to the table as a resource for innovation and democratized thinking. In this way, it reflects the mission and values of open communities. When you book your demo, ask for adjacent examples of CMS modules and workflows being utilized by similar associations as your own. This also includes transactional features, such as commerce for membership dues, etc. If you’re based in the UK and EU, Umbraco is already meeting data privacy and other compliance requirements, and has a strong sustainability strategy – so it checks many of the big boxes. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eIt would be wise to put them on your shortlist.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003chr /\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"upcoming-events\"\u003eUpcoming Events\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg style=\"width:34.15%\" src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/01/logo_jday_hor.png\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch4 id=\"joomladay-usa-2026\"\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.jdayusa.com/\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eJoomlaDay USA 2026\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/h4\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eApril 29 - May 2, 2026 – Delray Beach, Florida\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eBe part of the Joomla community in one of the most iconic cities in the world!
