the Human Touch on Hosting: Kinsta’s Matt Reid on Powering the Future of WordPress","intro":"The digital leader talks about the evolving landscape of open source, the value of relationships, AI’s transformative roadmap, and the importance of digital sovereignty in a changing world.","content":"\u003chr /\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eI love tech meetups. I go for the tech, but I’m really partial to the “meetup” part. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eThere’s usually a bit of imbibing on the docket. Craft beers are acceptable, but I much prefer mingling with craft coders and colliding around interesting topics. Like AI. Or that metaverse thing. It’s all on the table. I’m open to learning. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eI’ve had the chance to hit a few already this year, and at a smaller confab, I ran into a few digital agencies. One in particular, \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://webidextrous.com/\"\u003eWebidextrous\u003c/a\u003e – a full-service shop based in Winter Garden, Florida – reminded me that the heart of the WordPress community is alive and beating in these niche businesses. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAs CEO \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/crobertwatson/\"\u003eRob Watson\u003c/a\u003e told me, Webidextrous is helping real people with real business problems, and the relationship is still at the center of everything. As an ambassador of WordPress, he’s also actively participating in the ecosystem, penning his own brilliant reviews for \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://webidextrous.com/wordfence-wordpress-security-plugin-a-comprehensive-2025-review/\"\u003eplugins like Wordfence\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eWordPress effectively “scaffolds” the independence of local agencies like Rob's, and does so within a worldwide community of thousands. Over the years, the open source content management system has powered workloads small and large, from local to global. Today, it powers (roughly) 43% of all websites, 61% of the CMS market, and an ecosystem of over 60,000 free plugins and themes. No commercial platform can shake a stick at that.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eWordPress websites have to live somewhere, and as such, WordPress hosting has become ubiquitous. There’s a lot of choice in the market, much of it self-service and broadly accessible. It might be viewed by some as a commodity, and there’s some truth to that downstream. But at the enterprise level, focused hosting vendors have differentiated around key tenets of expertise and support, fomenting confidence with performance-tuned servers, uptime monitoring, firewalls, SLAs, and expert support. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eThis is where \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://kinsta.com/\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eKinsta\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/a\u003e is doubling down, providing a trusted resource for agencies and businesses that simplifies WordPress hosting. With over 230,000 customers around the world, including market-leading brands like TripAdvisor and NASA, Kinsta has consistently earned glowing reviews, particularly around the intangibles of support and relationships. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eThat last piece is critical in the evolving era of AI, where websites are changing. WordPress users and organizations are wading into promise and uncertainty. But most website owners are still struggling with the fundamentals, from migrations to edge caching. Security is a huge consideration, but so too are data ownership, governance, and digital sovereignty – topics that are making open source a more compelling and attractive play. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cfigure class=\"image image-style-align-center image_resized\" style=\"width:30.23%\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/02/image-1770850509724.png\" /\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"text-small\" style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003eKinsta CMO Matt Reid. Source: LinkedIn\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eI recently caught up with \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/mattreidsb/\"\u003eKinsta’s CMO Matt Reid,\u003c/a\u003e hoping to unpack the intersection of these trends. We talked about market shifts and the roiling impact of AI, but we also dug into Kinsta’s fervent focus on support – and how humans are at the center of everything.\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"differentiating-in-a-crowded-hosting-market\"\u003eDifferentiating in a crowded hosting market\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003eMatt brings solid experience from a strong run at \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://cmscritic.com/products/bigcommerce\"\u003eBigCommerce\u003c/a\u003e, one of the market’s leading SaaS e-commerce platforms. As its VP of Marketing, he drove everything from brand strategy to ABM programs, giving him a well-rounded perspective on the entire marketing lifecycle within the digital experience space.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eInjecting fresh perspective into Kinsta is part of Matt’s self-described value prop. As he told me, hosting is a greenfield category for him, but having a foundation in building partnerships is key to Kinsta’s strategy of cultivating its agency ecosystem. A big part of that is developing relationships with people, and Kinsta walks that talk with its own team. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“People have been here a long time,” Matt said, encapsulating the company’s fully remote workforce. “They really love the culture, the business, the customers. They love what we're doing on the product side. I mean, it's a cliché, but we treat them really, really well.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eInternally, Kinsta has cultivated a clear sense of purpose, targeting customers who treat their website as a mission-critical platform. That’s a bold position to take in a commodity space, but it speaks to Kinsta’s confidence and authority. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“We're not going to be for everybody,” Matt reinforced. “We're going to be for a certain set of the market that wants a professional-grade platform to run their business.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eBacking that up is a laser focus on performance, reliability, and managed operations. This comes from listening to customers and gauging their pain points around a host of key issues – and then delivering on the outcomes. And in a space where many vendors lead with infrastructure specs, Matt sees Kinsta’s “secret sauce” as a combination of technical excellence and real partnership.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“Speed is a key business metric,” he said. “So are things like ‘hands-off’ reliability. It should just work. All the updates, the scaling, the backup. We manage all of that. We know our niche, and we do it really well, and I think that we're not generic in that way. We're very authentic in how we treat our customers, and we back it up with solid technology.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAnd the technology speaks for itself. The \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://my.kinsta.com/login/\"\u003eMyKinsta\u003c/a\u003e dashboard is elegant, easy to navigate, and provides quick access to all critical resources. While it feels familiar and complementary to the native WordPress experience, it adds a layer of clarity, focus, and simplification. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cfigure class=\"image image-style-align-center image_resized\" style=\"width:83.26%\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/02/image-1770849185604.png\" alt=\"A screenshot of a computer\n\nAI-generated content may be incorrect.\" /\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"text-small\" style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003eSource: Kinsta website\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eMatt is bullish on WordPress – not just as a CMS, but as the core of an application and workflow platform. This is especially valuable as organizations rethink their website strategies and what tech they need in their stack. Open source presents a conduit to broader, community-driven innovation.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“WordPress isn’t going away,” he said. “There's always going to be additional widgets and plugins that are going to manifest. That's the great thing about open source. I've been involved with it before, and I really love the business model of getting my community connected with the direction and roadmap of where the technology is going.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cfigure class=\"image image-style-align-center image_resized\" style=\"width:52.48%\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/02/image-1770849185636.png\" alt=\"A screenshot of a phone\n\nAI-generated content may be incorrect.\" /\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"text-small\" style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003eSource: Kinsta website\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eComplementing the plugin ecosystem is Kinsta’s growing library of \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://kinsta.com/add-ons/\"\u003epremium add-ons,\u003c/a\u003e all accessible through an easy-to-use dashboard. This includes staging environments and dedicated servers, as well as advanced features like an \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://nginx.org/\"\u003enginx\u003c/a\u003e reverse proxy service or \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://redis.io/\"\u003eRedis\u003c/a\u003e in-memory data store for optimizing speed and performance. \u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"supporting-enterprise-compliance-and-digital-sovereignty\"\u003eSupporting enterprise compliance and digital sovereignty\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003eKinsta has its roots in the SMB and agency ecosystem, but Matt is seeing increased gravity from larger organizations wrestling with the diverse global challenges of compliance and governance across an evolving regulatory landscape. As he explained, these are key factors elevating the enterprise conversation.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“There are a lot of reasons why enterprises trust us, from global compliance and GDPR, SOC and ISO certification,” he said. “We’ve always been compliant because we want to be. And we do these things because it has an impact on the customer.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://trust.kinsta.com/\"\u003eKinsta’s Trust Center\u003c/a\u003e is perhaps the best example of how the company is investing in securing infrastructure, organizations, and products within its scope. There’s a deep commitment to data privacy and compliance controls, and that’s evident through its many badges, which include a host of badges and benchmarks. It’s as solid as solid can be.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eThe other part of Kinsta’s enterprise delivery is architectural. By leveraging a containerized approach, deployments are isolated by design, helping to ensure security and performance. There are also granular permissions to manage large teams of users. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eWhile Kinsta has the foundational components, Matt admits that their enterprise strategy is a long game, and that they’re still building momentum. “It takes time,” he said. “Moving from one hosting provider to another for enterprises is not something they're going to take lightly.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003chr /\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003ch4 style=\"text-align:center\" id=\"“there-are-a-lot-of-reasons-why-enterprises-trust-us,-from-global-compliance-and-gdpr,-soc-and-iso-certification.-we’ve-always-been-compliant-because-we-want-to-be.-and-we-do-these-things-because-it-has-an-impact-on-the-customer.”\"\u003e\u003ci\u003e\u003cmark class=\"marker-yellow\"\u003e“There are a lot of reasons why enterprises trust us, from global compliance and GDPR, SOC and ISO certification. We’ve always been compliant because we want to be. And we do these things because it has an impact on the customer.”\u003c/mark\u003e\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/h4\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003chr /\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAs social and geopolitical dynamics remain fluid, individuals, businesses, and even governments are seeking the safe harbor of sovereignty. This is surfacing in the re-emergence of local hosting, autonomous data centers, and even state-sanctioned LLMs \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://canxp.ai/maplept\"\u003elike Canada’s MaplePT\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAt our recent \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://cmscritic.com/beyond-the-gate-cms-kickoff-26-explored-the-ai-frontier-while-focusing-on-fundamentals\"\u003eBoye \u0026amp; Company CMS Kickoff 26\u003c/a\u003e conference, \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/karimmarucchi/\"\u003eKarim Marucchi of Crowd Favorite\u003c/a\u003e – an enterprise WordPress agency – talked about the evolving narrative around digital sovereignty and how open source CMSes are playing a critical role. Cementing trust has been a lingering atmospheric challenge for WordPress and its open source brethren, which was tested during \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://cmscritic.com/wp-engine-wins-an-injunction-against-automattic-is-the-wordpress-scorched-earth-campaign-over\"\u003ethe widely publicized Automattic debacle\u003c/a\u003e of late 2024. The crucible had a chilling effect on the entire ecosystem and raised questions about the security of its software supply chain.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eHosting was a big part of the quagmire, particularly around \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://cmscritic.com/products/wp-engine\"\u003eWP Engine’s\u003c/a\u003e managed WordPress as a business model. But the introduction of the \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://cmscritic.com/alls-fair-in-love-and-war-new-fair-package-manager-aims-to-bring-peace-to-the-wordpress-ecosystem\"\u003eFAIR Package\u003c/a\u003e and other resources has brought relative calm to the seas, demonstrating how the community, like nature, finds a way.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eKinsta is at the center of this, both on the open source side of the equation, as well as the vital infrastructure that supports it all. As Matt noted, there are critical factors that enable digital sovereignty on a global scale. This is where hosting providers have to meet data location requirements while delivering on the tenets with transparency and performance.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“If you’re a global business with 1,000 websites and a bunch of micro sites, what are you doing about data center infrastructure and support for EMEA versus APAC versus the US?” Matt said. “On top of that, what can you do to ensure that we are training digital sovereignty in such a way that you're going to be able to ensure it?”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eThese are big issues facing people, brands, and businesses alike, so there are no easy answers. But as a hosting provider, Matt sees Kinsta's role as an important one for ensuring the growth of open source across a connected world. \u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"the-ai-future:-powering-observability,-predictability,-and-more\"\u003eThe AI future: Powering observability, predictability, and more\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003eAI is at the center of every conversation right now, specifically on the agentic frontier, and \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.cheitgroup.com/blog/wordpress-2026-scalable-content-marketing\"\u003eWordPress is no exception.\u003c/a\u003e From content creation to image optimization to workflow management, AI is having an evolutionary impact on workflow automation, SEO, and even the human-AI collaboration within the WordPress ecosystem. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eThe introduction of \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://modelcontextprotocol.io/docs/getting-started/intro\"\u003eModel Context Protocol (MCP)\u003c/a\u003e as an adapter for intelligent agents is also enabling tools like \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://cmscritic.com/products/woocommerce\"\u003eWooCommerce\u003c/a\u003e to access website data and perform agentic tasks that are increasingly complex.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eWhile much of the industry’s AI conversation has focused on these top-line features, the hosting layer is also forging a new path with some interesting use cases for AI-enabled optimization. As Matt explained, Kinsta is drawing its own blueprints around AI’s operational leverage, particularly with its potential to reinforce observability, predictability, and incident prevention.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“We see AI behind the scenes, so to speak,” he commented. “There are some great monitoring and capacity planning activities that could happen with AI. And of course, improving observability. But the predictive piece of what AI can bring to the hosting market is really, really exciting, like anticipating traffic spikes.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAnd as complexity rises, Matt also sees AI automation as essential, not optional. “As you move into a platform play, you're moving into more complexity,” he said. “And with complexity comes a lot of headaches. If you don't automate the manual in a complex world, you don't necessarily have the skillset available in the workforce to be able to adapt to what those changes are. I think AI can be really critical in that world.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eUltimately, the goal is to solve problems before customers ever feel the impact.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“What AI is going to allow us to do is fine-tune everything,” Matt codified. “We'll be able to solve problems before they exist or manifest themselves where the customer sees an impact.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"why-human-support-still-matters-(and-is-a-revenue-driver)\"\u003eWhy human support still matters (and is a revenue driver)\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003eThe conversation eventually turned to support, a quintessential part of the hosting experience. As a practitioner who has used a range of platforms to power my own WordPress sites, everything from GoDaddy to AWS, I’ve always relied on help in a pinch – especially in the days when accessing a cPanel and modifying MX records were rife with peril.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eI reminded Matt about the legendary \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rackspace_Technology\"\u003eRackspace\u003c/a\u003e, and how its “Fanatical Support” was once the industry standard. Of course, that was before the hyperscalers exerted significant competition and poor restructuring impacted its operations. In truth, it never recovered after \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://strategicrationale.substack.com/p/from-cloud-to-clutter-apollos-failed\"\u003eApollo’s failed buyout.\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eMatt believes support is one of the strongest threads for Kinsta. With a 98% satisfaction rating, it’s not just window dressing – it’s a core differentiator and, perhaps more importantly, a growth driver. Those are tall orders to back up, but he pointed out how they consistently bridge the gaps that other vendors miss. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“I hear a lot of talk about a customer having issues, whether it’s needing an upgrade, or moving a website somewhere, and it going into a little bit of a ‘black hole’ with their vendor,” he said. “And we've certainly differentiated ourselves in the space, not just providing excellent infrastructure and scalability and performance, but the people to back it up.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eThat promise is acutely evident with \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://kinsta.com/wordpress-hosting/migration/\"\u003eKinsta’s migration services.\u003c/a\u003e They make the move fast, easy, and free, with zero downtime. They also offer malware cleanup, enterprise-grade security, and the promise of instant speed improvements of up to 200%. They can expedite it in as little as 8 hours, or you can DIY using its \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://kinsta.com/docs/wordpress-hosting/wordpress-migrations/migrate-guru/\"\u003eMigrate Guru,\u003c/a\u003e a free plugin from WordPress.org.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eAs Matt pointed out, the real key to success and satisfaction is Kinsta’s dedicated team of in-house experts, who go beyond a simple lift and shift. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“I think a big differentiator is the fact that we have real humans on the other side of the line throughout the migration process, focusing on the scalability and performance of your site,” he explained. “We have experts in WordPress at Kinsta, and they’re here to handhold our customers throughout any kind of migration, as well as upgrades, backups, add-ons, security patches, and more.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eFor Matt, Kinsta’s support philosophy is part of how the company is reshaping the industry and its expectations. Excellence, growth, and credibility are the central pillars of its promise – and that’s translating into growth.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“It becomes a revenue bond,” he said.\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"what’s-next\"\u003eWhat’s next\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003eAs I said, websites are evolving in the AI era. Some question their long-term viability in a world where answer engines are hijacking traffic. But LLMs need websites, and brands need a stage for owning the customer experience. And for the vast majority of the market, the web continues to be the most important channel for transacting with the world.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eBut websites themselves have indeed transformed, becoming applications with a multitude of API-connected services and integrations. There’s more potential – but also more to worry about with security, compliance, and performance.  \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eLooking ahead, Matt sees demand coalescing around more sophisticated lifecycle and workflow support – especially for teams treating their site as a true application platform. That implies tighter integration with broader delivery and release processes. These are places where Kinsta can have a meaningful impact.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e“A lot of our customers want to be able to stage out specific environments,” he explained. “We're hearing things like, ‘How can we manage the ability to perform testing frameworks before we go into production?’ There's a big market need there, just with regard to the website as a critical component. It \u003ci\u003ebecomes\u003c/i\u003e the platform.”\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eOn the application front, Kinsta is also steadily innovating and expanding its core value, particularly on the development side of the ledger. In 2024, the company launched a PaaS solution called \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://sevalla.com/\"\u003eSevalla\u003c/a\u003e that effectively eliminates the challenges of managing infrastructure for building and deploying apps. This includes all the essentials, from app and object storage to database and static site hosting – all with top-notch security certifications. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cimg style=\"width:60.01%\" src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/02/image-1770849185591.png\" alt=\"A white background with black and orange text\n\nAI-generated content may be incorrect.\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"text-small\" style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003eSource: Kinsta\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eWhat I love about Sevalla is how it simplifies the complexities of app hosting by mitigating the \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://kubernetes.io/\"\u003eKubernetes\u003c/a\u003e headaches (and trust me, they are numerous). You can deploy from any source, including public or private Git repos or \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.docker.com/\"\u003eDocker\u003c/a\u003e images and registries. It’s pipeline-centric, and appealing to DevOps teams looking to run their own stack with access to a global network of data centers and \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://cmscritic.com/products/cloudflare\"\u003eCloudflare\u003c/a\u003e servers. \u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"why-it-matters\"\u003eWhy it matters\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003eThe hosting landscape is highly competitive, and commoditization is a persistent threat. But Kinsta’s WordPress focus – combined with its strong technical prowess and dynamite support model – is putting real wind in its sails, particularly with enterprises that are embracing WordPress and open source. Kinsta’s data center footprint is robust, and its security and stability offer a solid foundation.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eWordPress agencies are a loyal bunch, and with so much riding on performance and customer satisfaction, having reliable partnerships is key. Kinsta seems to have a steady pulse on the community, driving more in-person engagement to help cultivate relationships. It’s a long-game strategy that appears to be paying off.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eOn the AI arc, WordPress is continuing to expand its offerings, both at the core level and via its plugin ecosystem. Kinsta’s own vision for applying AI behind the scenes – targeting predictive capabilities and incident prevention – could drive even greater value and differentiation as they manifest.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan class=\"text-big\"\u003e\u003cmark class=\"marker-yellow\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMy recommendation: \u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/mark\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eKinsta really delivers on a number of fronts, including ease of use and migration. Everything is here, from native Cloudflare CDN to analytics and monitoring. The documentation is really solid (\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://kinsta.com/docs/\"\u003eI’ve checked it out in detail\u003c/a\u003e), covering all the essentials from site creation through setting up staging environments. There's a ton of runway for customization, so keep that in mind. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eManaging your WordPress workloads should be a snap using the MyKinsta dashboard, which is lightweight and incredibly easy to use. \u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://kinsta.com/pricing/\"\u003ePricing is ultra-clear,\u003c/a\u003e with free tiers to test drive and flexible plans. Agencies have their own team-based pricing models, which makes it an attractive play.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eWith 24/7/365 expert support, Kinsta brings a “human touch” not just to support, but to every aspect of its business – and customer testimonials codify that. ","content":"\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://cmscritic.com/critics/bmckeiver\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBrian McKeiver\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e\u003ci\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e is Co-Owner of \u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.bizstream.com\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBizStream\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e,\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e\u003ci\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e a digital agency in Grand Rapids, MI, USA. He’s been in the CMS space for over 18 years and is recognized as a Microsoft Azure MVP in AI and Cloud, Kentico MVP, Kontent.ai MVP, and a CMS Critic contributor. \u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003chr /\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eOver the past few decades, I’ve seen firsthand how the CMS world has changed rapidly to meet the evolving needs of organizations and digital marketing teams. From the beginning, when teams were creating their own CMS from scratch, to the move to proprietary platforms, to World Wide Web Consortium (W3C) standards, to handling localization, mobile responsiveness, SEO, personalization, GDPR, WCAG accessibility, and a chatbot and cookie banner on every site, change has been constant.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eHowever, that pace of change is almost nothing compared to how much and how fast Artificial Intelligence (AI) is taking the world by storm. Platform vendors, agencies, consultants, analysts, and customers are all scrambling to try and stay on top of the AI arms race that we are all in now. As we start 2026, everyone is in the same boat of, “How can I figure this out?”, “What do I do next?”, and “How can I stay ahead?”\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"trends-for-platforms,-agencies,-and-customers-in-2026\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eTrends for Platforms, Agencies, and Customers in 2026\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eTrends that I see all include the letters “A” and “I”. You cannot look anywhere in the CMS, development technology, or digital marketing worlds without seeing or hearing about AI. It dominates the headlines, and end customers, agencies, and platform vendors alike are craving it.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eMy point was actually proven on stage at the recent \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://cmscritic.com/beyond-the-gate-cms-kickoff-26-explored-the-ai-frontier-while-focusing-on-fundamentals\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210, 75%, 60%)\"\u003eBoye \u0026amp; Company annual CMS Kickoff conference\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e in St. Petersburg, Florida. Just about every session and every CMS platform demo at the conference was all about AI. Agentic AI and the idea of AI agents taking over content operations was a huge topic; Generative Engine Optimization (GEO) was the second-largest topic discussed; MCP Servers (a way for LLMs to communicate with outside systems, third-party APIs, and external tools) came in third. Digital sovereignty was also brought up a few times because having control over your data is crucial to getting the most value out of AI and having an AI advantage.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eIt wasn’t just the CMS Kickoff conference, though. I’ve had similar experiences at other large national technology conferences, where every session and every demo was on AI. I’ve kept track of very recent insights from Satya Nadella, CEO of Microsoft, on how AI must evolve from standalone models to real systems with real effects. Frankly, I’ve been totally blown away by Vercel’s latest open source agent skill ecosystem growth (over 10,000 new AI agent skills added in the first 72 hours on \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"http://skills.sh\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eskills.sh\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e). \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eThis doesn’t even take into account this past January’s announcement of \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://claude.com/blog/cowork-research-preview\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eClaude Cowork\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e being created fully by AI and launched within 1 week by the team at Anthropic. Cowork allows non-technical people to dive into the work of having AI agents complete everyday tasks for them with almost zero effort. AI truly is in every facet of what we do now.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eTo bring it back to the CMS space, though, a consistent arms race has really been going on for about the last 18 months or so, and will continue into 2026 and beyond. Optimizely has \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.optimizely.com/ai/\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eOpal\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e,\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e an AI agent orchestration platform. Sitecore has rebranded to \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"http://sitecore.ai\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eSitecore.ai\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eand now bills itself as the next-generation DXP for the AI era. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eKentico has \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.kentico.com/platform/aira\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eARIA\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e and \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://docs.kentico.com/guides/development/kenticopilot\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eKentiCopilot\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e initiatives (more about this further below). Storyblok has \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.storyblok.com/lp/strata\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eStrata\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e and \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.storyblok.com/lp/flowmotion\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eFlowMotion\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e for vectorization of content and native AI automations. Kontent.ai is moving forward quickly with its built-in AI Agent to be a leader in \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://kontent.ai/features/agentic-cms/\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eAgentic CMS\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e.\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e Umbraco has a pretty robust\u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://umbraco.com/blog/unveiling-umbraco-mcp-server/\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#1155cc\"\u003e \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eMCP Server\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e for content creation and migrations. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eAdobe's new \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://experienceleague.adobe.com/en/docs/experience-cloud-ai/experience-cloud-ai/agents/agent-orchestrator\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003esuite of AI tools\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e launched for agent orchestration, and it has out-of-the-box agents like the Audience Agent, Journey Agent, and Experimentation Agent. Shopify and Salesforce Commerce have gone all in on Agentic Commerce and the new \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.shopify.com/ucp\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eUniversal Commerce Protocol\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e (UCP). I could keep going too, but I think that’s enough.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eThe goal of all of this is to drastically increase the efficiency and speed at which digital marketing teams can operate at. AI will supercharge marketers to do more at scale. That’s why all of this is such an exciting trend.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cfigure class=\"image image-style-align-center image_resized\" style=\"width:88.27%\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/02/brian-mckeiver-agentic-ai-agencies.jpg\" /\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\u003ch2 id=\"the-effect-on-agencies\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eThe Effect on Agencies\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eOverall, it is a tumultuous world for digital agencies in 2026. Most agencies, including my own at \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.bizstream.com/\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eBizStream\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e,\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e are watching all of this very carefully. While I used the word “exciting” previously, when you shift the perspective to look at it from our standpoint, to be honest, the word that comes to mind is “terrifying”. I say that because the world of Agentic CMS and AI agents has the very real potential to completely upend the way we have done business for the last many years.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eAs agents get more sophisticated and can do more of what marketers want, that could mean that marketers might not need to rely on agency support as much. Marketers can just vibe market and vibe code up that next campaign landing page with personalized variants, that next brand refresh and UX update, or email campaign now, right? In my opinion, some of that might be true, but not all. There will still need to be a human in the loop.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eWe’ve seen this idea happen in the development space for some time now. When ChatGPT and GitHub Copilot came out in roughly 2023/24, every headline was that software developers and software engineers everywhere would become obsolete. That has not been the case. We need skilled developers to call out AI where AI is wrong, and it is wrong often. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eHowever, in the last three months, with the release of the latest models like Opus 4.6, developers are more and more becoming orchestrators of coding agents and less and less writers of syntax. It is a change that some developers welcome, and at the same time makes some developers very nervous. Agencies cannot ignore the fact that the way technical teams build software is completely changing.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eIt’s not just software developers and technical users that this trend is massive on. This week, I had a chance to participate in a mastermind session of local technology leaders in West Michigan. I happen to sit at the same table as the director of digital marketing at a very large local organization. We spent over 30 minutes talking about where he is at with his digital strategy, his main branded site, and all the native apps that connect to it. They had just chosen a new CMS to replatform to, and to my surprise, they are all-in on agentic development, including him directly. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eTo prove how much he believes in the future of agentic development and how it is the only way forward, over a weekend, he personally built a component using Claude Code, matching the requirements and design system. He also did his first-ever pull request into the source code repository for the team’s main project. The team was shocked. His work proved a point: that agentic development to create real-world components was possible. The next day, they had a few more components built using AI by a few software engineers on the project. A little while later, they had many components developed using Claude code and are now moving on to the next phase of the project.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eThis director is not a professional coder; he is a director who wants to show his people that this is the future. In my opinion, those actions are quite impressive for a non-software developer.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eHere’s the most interesting part of this story. He told me it took over 3 years to build the last iteration of their full digital experience platform and all the commerce and native apps it required with a full team of engineers. This month, he has given that team a deadline of completing the full migration to the new CMS, including a rebuild in a new stack, within the next 8 months. Yes, he expects, and is pushing to, turn what used to take over 3 years of effort into 8 months of effort (without any agency help, by the way).\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eThis drastic level of change for Agentic CMS and agentic development, or evolution as I like to think about it, requires agencies to rethink how they deliver value, how they charge for services, how they go to market, and how they keep up with the competition. I’m shocked that in 2026, some agencies are still ignoring this massive trend and continuing to do business as if it were 2020. Frankly, this is what is keeping me up at night: \u003ci\u003ehow can we re-tool our whole organization in such a short time?\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eLuckily, I’m surrounded by a brilliant team and have some key partnerships with platform vendors. We are pushing forward and figuring it out. We have our own code to design workflow now that lets us take the user stories and requirements for our client’s projects, marry that with design systems in Figma, and let agents create code, components, and widgets inside of the chosen CMS platform. It’s pretty remarkable to see it all work. It’s also nice to be able to participate in the CMS Experts group and see what others are doing in this space as well. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"why-bizstream-as-an-agency-still-chooses-kentico\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eWhy BizStream as an Agency Still Chooses Kentico\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eI am most likely slightly biased, and I think it is fair to acknowledge that, but my agency really likes where Kentico is at in 2026. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eAt BizStream, we have partnered with many CMS, DXP, and E-commerce platforms over the years, but throughout all of that, we've been working with Kentico the whole time, over 17 years straight, in fact. The technology has always been solid and in our wheelhouse in terms of being based on the Microsoft Azure and .NET stacks. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eKentico’s main flagship hybrid headless DXP, \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.kentico.com/platform\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eXperience by Kentico\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e,\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e is performing incredibly well for us, and our customers love it. The people behind the product are quite dedicated and care about it passionately. The commercial and partner teams support our agency when we need it very well, especially with transparent pricing and effective partner communication. Customer support and service have always been top-notch; in fact, they went above and beyond yet again a few weeks ago when helping me troubleshoot a live production issue in the middle of the night.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eFrom a product standpoint, and what matters highly to BizStream, is that Kentico has always been at the forefront of modernization. \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.1888pressrelease.com/kentico-introduces-windows-azure-competency-pr-294097.html\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eKentico CMS was the first .NET CMS to be certified in the Azure cloud back in 2011\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e.\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e The CMS was one of the first .NET platforms to embrace the MVC development style when it first became a part of the .NET framework, and the CMS/DXP has led the way in terms of supporting the modern \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"http://asp.net\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eASP.NET\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e Core story and .NET 10. Even though modernization is not always where marketing teams want to spend their budgets, we think this is key to being able to be innovative in a very crowded space.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eOther than those factors, Kentico has embraced the idea of agentic development and AI agents for quite some time now. As an MVP, my team and I have had early access to Kentico’s AI strategy and tools. We’ve been able to combine that with our \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.bizstream.com/technology/kentico/\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eWeb Accelerator for Kentico\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e starter template and are seeing some impressive results. Let’s dive into that strategy a bit more.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"kentico’s-ai-vision\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eKentico’s AI Vision\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eI've had long conversations with the team at Kentico, including the head of product, Debbie Tucek, and CEO Dominik Pinter, about where Kentico sees the future of CMS over the past 24 months. I appreciate the prudent path that they have taken and the vision that they have for the future.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eWhile some platforms bolted AI right onto an existing aging stack, Kentico took a different approach. They didn’t just add a chatbot interface on a new screen with text generation and summary; they ignored that step. Kentico wants to use AI to fundamentally attack the two hardest challenges in digital agencies and customers: operational efficiency (making the process of content management go faster) and technical friction (quicker builds, cheaper upgrades, and continuous modernization). Responsible use of AI was also talked about at every turn in these discussions as well.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eInside the Xperience by Kentico ecosystem, there are two large new umbrellas of functionality to tackle the two challenges. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cfigure class=\"image image-style-align-center image_resized\" style=\"width:89.47%\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/02/image-1770648188813.png\" /\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"aira-for-marketers-\u0026amp;-the-aira-agentic-marketing-suite\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eAIRA for Marketers \u0026amp; the AIRA Agentic Marketing Suite\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eThe first large umbrella of features is AIRA, short for Artificial Intelligence Recommendations and Assistance. AIRA originally appeared in the early fall of 2025. It was introduced as a helper utility within the CMS admin tool. It has matured since then, and today AIRA is Xperience by Kentico's native AI toolset built to help content admins automate creation and deployment of content. It’s now been branded as the \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.kentico.com/platform/agentic-marketing-suite\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eAIRA Agentic Marketing Suite\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eThe AIRA Agentic Marketing Suite is still directly inside of the CMS admin tool, right at the fingertips of admin users. It is a reference to a set of out of the box Ai agents. The vision is that AIRA's AI teammates will be able to support digital marketing planning, content creation, content testing, and content optimization so ideas turn into measurable results, faster, and convert more. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003ch4 id=\"aira-smart-assistant-\u0026amp;-ai-agent\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAIRA Smart Assistant \u0026amp; AI Agent\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h4\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eAIRA acts as a helpful assistant and is represented by AI agents. It can answer questions about Kentico and lead a content editor to the right place within the system to get up to speed faster. It also gives insights on the performance of content in the system. AIRA can even help out with content creation and automated management of content. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cfigure class=\"image image-style-align-center image_resized\" style=\"width:88.93%\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/02/image-1770648187613.png\" /\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"text-small\" style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003eSource: Brian McKeiver via Kentico\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eThere is also a set of governance and control for how it is implemented. If an organization wants to use AIRA, they can enable it with one simple check box to turn it on. If an organization doesn’t want to step into the AI-powered world, AIRA is just as easily disabled with a simple uncheck of a checkbox. There are also further roles and permissions that can be applied to what administrative users can and cannot do. I think that this is a responsible approach and speaks to the Kentico leadership team’s approach to AI enablement.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003ch4 id=\"aira-specific-features\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAIRA Specific Features\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h4\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eMy favorite feature of AIRA is the ability to \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://docs.kentico.com/guides/digital-marketing/work-with-multilingual/automate-translations-with-aira\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003etranslate pages\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e,\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e emails, and content items with an LLM. You can also maintain the same tone and terminology of the translated content with configurable translation rules. One key aspect of this new feature is that it can automatically detect all the dependent or child components that make up a page and ensure those are translated too. That prevents the editor from accidentally missing a child component or random asset that makes up the entire full page.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eAI translation alone is a highly sought-after feature by many of my customers. It also tends to be an expensive feature. AIRA does make this much easier. AIRA credits are consumed by this and other specific AI features to be transparent, though.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cfigure class=\"image image-style-align-center image_resized\" style=\"width:88.74%\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/02/image-1770648187531.png\" /\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"text-small\" style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003eSource: Brian McKeiver via Kentico\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eOther specific features of AIRA include automatic image focal points, auto tagging of assets to a taxonomy, and smart asset alt text generation. These are small things, but add up to all be quite helpful.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eLastly, text fields can be configured to allow generative text capabilities like rewrites from brand tone, shorten to be more concise, and other ChatGPT-like writing features.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eThe specific features that are AI-enabled are nice, but the real unlock of AIRA is the AI agents that it ships with.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003ch4 id=\"aira-as-an-agent(s)\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAIRA as an Agent(s)\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h4\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eThe AIRA Agentic Marketing Suite includes a Content Strategist Agent and Customer Journey Optimization Specialist in preview. The first production release of the Agents will be available in the upcoming February update to the platform. More agents and ways to even look at your entire agent ecosystem are planned. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eThe Content Strategist Agent thinks about your content ecosystem as a whole and not just independent paragraphs where you have to explain the full context. It can analyze your existing content to identify gaps and provide recommendations on what to create next. It acts as a protector of your organization’s brand tone, maintaining editorial guidelines to ensure every piece is coherent and strategic.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eThe Customer Journey Optimization Specialist Agent shows where Customer Journeys in Kentico are working and not working. It can clearly highlight where users drop off, but offer support in explaining why the drop off happens and/or how to improve the performance of the journey. Marketers will receive contextual, actionable recommendations directly within the Customer Journeys application inside the CMS.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eAround Q1 and into Q2 of this year, another agent – the Campaign Manager agent – is coming. Instead of starting every campaign from scratch, it will recall historical campaigns and know performance results. It turns campaign management into a continuous learning system, ensuring you don't repeat past mistakes. It can help build on what has succeeded before.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eThrough a conversational interface, marketers will be able to collaborate with AIRA to create a campaign brief, turn it directly into an executable campaign, and continuously validate progress. AIRA will check whether assets are prepared as planned and whether customer journey results align with the goals defined in the brief. The result is enhanced and easier campaign orchestration.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eI’ve used these tools and seen them since the beginning. I think our customers are very much going to appreciate the time saved by leveraging these AI features and agents.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"kenticopilot-for-developers\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eKentiCopilot for Developers\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eCloser to my heart, as I have a highly technical background, is the second main umbrella of Kentico’s AI strategy: \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://docs.kentico.com/x/kenticocopilot_guides\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eKentiCopilot\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e.\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e KentiCopilot is not a single feature but a suite of tools designed for developers and implementation partners to enable agentic development. There are multiple parts to it.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cfigure class=\"image image-style-align-center image_resized\" style=\"width:91.69%\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/02/image-1770648187393.png\" /\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"text-small\" style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003eSource: Brian McKeiver\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003ch4 id=\"kentico-mcp-server(s)\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eKentico MCP Server(s)\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h4\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eKentico's first MCP server was announced, under the KentiCopilot umbrella, and made live after \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.mcbeev.com/kentico-connection-miami-2024-recap\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003elast fall's annual Kentico Connection\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e event. The documentation MCP Server was all about knowing up-to-date Kentico knowledge and being grounded to the new Xperience by Kentico platform documentation. This ensured no legacy documentation, research, forums, blogs, etc. etc. about the legacy versions of Kentico would cause hallucinations. Accurate information helps new and seasoned Kentico developers get the right information faster.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eA newer MCP Server, launched in December 2025 is the \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://community.kentico.com/blog/xperience-by-kentico-refresh-december-11-2025#agent-driven-content-type-management-with-the-content-types-mcp-server\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eContent types MCP Server\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e for Kentico. It enables developers to work with content types in Kentico using LLMs. It supports operations such as creating content types, creating reusable field schemas, as well as editing, reading, and deleting them. You can change the entire shape of your content model easily with this tool. The MCP Server is also useful for data migrations and initial imports of content from CSV files, JSON files, or other CMSs.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003ch4 id=\"custom-widget-builder-agent\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCustom Widget Builder Agent\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h4\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eNow available at GitHub, Kentico has also released a set of \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://community.kentico.com/blog/xperience-by-kentico-refresh-december-11-2025#prompting-success-with-ai-agent-widget-generation\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003ecustom instructions\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003e for how you can use Claude, Cursor, VS Code, or other code editors to use agents to write front-end code for you. Being able to go from a prompt to having finished Razor views that are registered as Xperience by Kentico Page Builder widgets is incredibly powerful. This has long been possible in the JavaScript framework world, but in .NET this is a bit harder to get correct. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eThis aspect of KentiCopilot is the most exciting aspect to me. Kentico partners and customers have longed for the ability to generate the front end of the solution much faster than writing it custom. Enabling a custom widget builder agent on a project is game-changing. We have been using a version of this and seen it completely accelerate our development workflow. I cannot recommend enough that Kentico developers immerse themselves in this repository, especially if they are new to agentic development.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003ch4 id=\"kentico-migration-toolkit-enhancements\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eKentico Migration Toolkit Enhancements\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h4\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eOne of the biggest headaches in the DXP world is the upgrade cycle. Moving from legacy versions (like Kentico 13) to a modern stack has historically been complex. It requires a large amount of effort and time. It slows down marketing teams.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eThe latest updates to KentiCopilot specifically target this friction point with AI-assisted code upgrades. These tools assist developers in migrating code and content models from older versions to Xperience by Kentico. It lowers the cost of an upgrade, turning what used to be a daunting migration into a manageable evolution. As of January 2025, there are even some supported code migration capabilities. This takes the form of more custom instructions inside of the GitHub repository for how AI coding assistants can migrate some of the live site presentation logic.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cfigure class=\"image image-style-align-center image_resized\" style=\"width:42.81%\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/02/image-1770648187099.png\" /\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"text-small\" style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003e\u003ci\u003eSource: Kentico\u003c/i\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp style=\"text-align:center\"\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eNow, I’ve been a part of the Kentico Migration Toolkit offering since the beginning of it and was one of the first people to use it live in production. It has always been about migrating the data of legacy versions of the CMS to the Xperience by Kentico. Now with KentiCopilot, the story is different. Using the newest agentic techniques, Kentico is attempting to assist as much as possible with migrating your code as well.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eThe tool is good, and I do recommend it, but it does still have a few gaps in the total service it offers. Don’t get me wrong, though; it does deliver the savings that it promised when compared to having no tooling to start with. Depending on the scenario, it can still be better to write custom migration tooling to support what the Kentico Migration Toolkit does.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"where-kentico-differentiates\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eWhere Kentico Differentiates\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eKentico is dogfooding AIRA and KentiCopilot as much as they can. They use KentiCopilot internally to build their own digital properties, such as their demo sites and the new Community Portal. This means they feel the friction of development and pass this information on to us agencies to hopefully improve the process, and stop any AI hallucinations that may occur.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eThis approach can be invisible to an end client, but it directly impacts project costs and timelines. If AI can reduce the \"grunt work\" of development by 33% or more, that translates directly to faster launch times and more budget available for more high-value strategic tasks rather than just getting the basics right.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eHowever, there are challenges with this strategy. For instance, the pricing model of how AI features in AIRA will be metered and is not yet publicly released. Pricing has caused pain for Kentico (and many other vendors in the space) for over 6 months now. Because it is all so new, almost all platform vendors are trying to figure out what kind of cost they will have, and how to fairly charge customers. This reminds me of how Microsoft first released Copilot to only a select number of enterprise clients, and did not really reveal its pricing to the rest of the world.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eAnother challenge is how Kentico will differentiate itself against the competition. As I mentioned above, almost every CMS/DXP/Headless platform is rushing to add these types of features. For me, the differentiator for Kentico is the order in which they are tackling the AI problem. As I said, many platforms are leading with flashy AI features aimed purely at marketers. The underlying developer experience remains archaic and manual. Kentico has taken a foundational approach by reducing technical friction. That decision matters because the speed of delivery still dictates whether AI-powered features can actually reach production and deliver value.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eBy focusing on autonomous marketing agentics, agentic development, modernization, and tooling for customers, Kentico is effectively multiplying the impact of AI. Agencies can deliver more reliably, customers can iterate more frequently, and AI features stop being experimental add-ons and instead become part of standard operations.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eKentico’s differentiation is also cultural as much as it is technical. Their product leadership has been transparent about what is ready, what is still evolving, and where customers should be cautious. In an era where AI hype is everywhere, that honesty builds long-term trust with agencies and enterprise customers alike.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"impact-at-bizstream\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eImpact at BizStream\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eWe've seen real-world impact on efficiency at BizStream. Implementation tasks that used to take 16 hours are now taking 30 minutes when orchestrated correctly. I’m not going to lie; to set up all this has taken a few months. The context you provide is super important to agents. You should give it very specific instructions, including good examples and patterns to match and examples to NOT follow. You should feed it exactly how your team works, handles code conventions, and tests for quality. If the result is not working the way you expect it, give that back to the AI and explain why it’s wrong. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eThis is a repetitive pattern, but worth getting the details correct. Utilizing AI agents has also opened up our technical team to move more into the strategic work and work less on the syntax work. Our engineers are becoming orchestrators. AI is supercharging them to do more than they could before.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eAll of these changes have also opened up new challenges for us. The market is expecting to see some of the efficiencies passed on to the customer. We are having to rethink how we price our services to meet that new demand. We are also having to create new materials for how we sell services, and update our marketing to acknowledge the new way that we are delivering. All of this is not quite public yet, but I am excited to see the results and can’t wait to launch it all. We are truly orchestrating the next generation of our agency.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch2 id=\"conclusion\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eConclusion\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eIn my opinion and prediction, agentic AI, AI agents, agentic CMS, agentic marketing practices, and agentic development practices are all here to stay. No matter whether you are a platform vendor, agency, end customer, consultant, or analyst, you need to be exploring and experimenting with how AI can help you go faster and deliver more.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eWhat is becoming increasingly clear is that success in this new era will not come from simply bolting AI onto existing processes. It requires rethinking workflows, investing in the right foundations, and keeping humans firmly in the loop. Organizations that treat AI as a power tool rather than a rusty old hammer will be the ones to succeed in this new world.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#000000\"\u003eFor me, as an agency owner, it truly is the most exciting and most terrifying thing to ever happen all at once. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003chr /\u003e\u003ch3 id=\"upcoming-events\"\u003eUpcoming Events\u003c/h3\u003e\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cimg style=\"width:34.15%\" src=\"https://cmscritic.com/ms-content/uploads/2026/01/logo_jday_hor.png\" /\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003ch4 id=\"joomladay-usa-2026\"\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://www.jdayusa.com/\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:hsl(210,75%,60%)\"\u003eJoomlaDay USA 2026\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/h4\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eApril 29 - May 2, 2026 – Delray Beach, Florida\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eBe part of the Joomla community in one of the most iconic cities in the world!
